1.5em">\n\n<tbody><tr>\n<td><b>Map all coordinates using:</b> <a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/osm4wiki/cgi-bin/wiki/wiki-osm.pl?project=en&amp;article=South_Somerset">OpenStreetMap</a>&#160;\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td><b>Download coordinates as:</b> <a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/kmlexport?article=South_Somerset">KML</a>&#160;<b>&#183;</b>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://tripgang.com/kml2gpx/http%3A%2F%2Ftools.wmflabs.org%2Fkmlexport%3Farticle%3DSouth_Somerset?gpx=1">GPX</a>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p><b>South Somerset</b> is a <a href="/wiki/Non-metropolitan_district" title="Non-metropolitan district">local government district</a> in <a href="/wiki/Somerset" title="Somerset">Somerset</a>, <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>.\n</p><p>The South Somerset district covers and area of 370 square miles (958&#160;km<sup>2</sup>)<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> ranging from the borders with <a href="/wiki/Devon" title="Devon">Devon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wiltshire" title="Wiltshire">Wiltshire</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dorset" title="Dorset">Dorset</a> to the edge of the <a href="/wiki/Somerset_Levels" title="Somerset Levels">Somerset Levels</a>. It has a population of approximately 158,000.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> The administrative centre of the district is <a href="/wiki/Yeovil" title="Yeovil">Yeovil</a>.\n</p><p>The district was formed on 1 April 1974, and was originally known as <b>Yeovil</b>, adopting its present name in 1985.  It was formed by the merger of the <a href="/wiki/Municipal_borough" title="Municipal borough">municipal boroughs</a> of <a href="/wiki/Chard,_Somerset" title="Chard, Somerset">Chard</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yeovil" title="Yeovil">Yeovil</a>, along with <a href="/wiki/Crewkerne" title="Crewkerne">Crewkerne</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ilminster" title="Ilminster">Ilminster</a> <a href="/wiki/Urban_district_(Great_Britain_and_Ireland)" title="Urban district (Great Britain and Ireland)">urban districts</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Chard_Rural_District" title="Chard Rural District">Chard Rural District</a>, <a href="/wiki/Langport_Rural_District" title="Langport Rural District">Langport Rural District</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wincanton_Rural_District" title="Wincanton Rural District">Wincanton Rural District</a> and <a href="/wiki/Yeovil_Rural_District" title="Yeovil Rural District">Yeovil Rural District</a>.\n</p><p>The Council covers the whole of the <a href="/wiki/Yeovil_(UK_Parliament_constituency)" title="Yeovil (UK Parliament constituency)">Yeovil constituency</a>, and part of <a href="/wiki/Somerton_and_Frome_(UK_Parliament_constituency)" title="Somerton and Frome (UK Parliament constituency)">Somerton and Frome</a>.\n</p><p>It is currently <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Democrats_(UK)" title="Liberal Democrats (UK)">Liberal Democrat</a> controlled, and has <a href="/wiki/Beacon_Council_(award)" title="Beacon Council (award)">Beacon Council</a> status.\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc"><input type="checkbox" role="button"
